 ajay makanne anya udhaaharan dete hue kaha ki bade dukh kii baat he pichley 6 maheene se aap party kii dilli sarkaar main koi bhi aisa mantri nahi he jo dalit varg kaa pratinidhitiv karata ho
 Whereas during the recent election campaign of Punjab, Delhi Chief Minister Shri Arvind Kejriwal had misled the people of Punjab and said that he will make Deputy Chief Minister from Dalit class in Punjab
 bijepi ne saaf kiya he ki meghalaya main gomance par pratibandh nahin hoga
 The party alleged that the Congress was 'misleading' the people on the issue to gain political mileage ahead of next year's elections
 rajya bijepi ke adhyaksh shibun lingadoh ne kaha ki centre ne meghalaya mengomancepar pratibandh nahin lagaaya he
 He alleged that the May 23 notification calls for regularization of animal markets, including the functioning of cattle markets and dealing with animals brought for trade
 bijepi pravaktaa jee lingadoh ne bayaan jari kar kaha ki party ne ‘spasht kar diya he ki purvottar rajyon main ise (gomance pratibandh) lagu nahin kiya jayega
 Livestock is a matter of state
 is par rajyon ko nirnay karnaa he
 'he said that the beef ban would not apply in the state
 unhone kaha ki gomance par pratibandh lagaana na to acchhee aarthik pahal he na hi samvidhan sammat he
 In the 39th match of IPL season 10, Pune Supergiant defeated Gujarat Lions by 5 wickets
 162 ranon ke lakshya kaa peechha karte hue pune superjyant ne 19
 Scored 167 runs for 5 wickets in 5 overs
 ben stokes ne shandaar shatak lagaakar pune ko jeet dilaai
 Ben Stokes (103) scored the first century of his IPL career
 pune kii paripune kii shuruyaat kharaab rahi thi
 The team lost their two crucial wickets in the very first over, after which Stokes won Pune by playing a great inning
 stokes ne 63 ball par 103 ran kii tufaani ining kheli
 In this, he hit 7 fours and 6 sixes
 is dauraan unka strike rate 163
 49 stokes ke alaava emes dhoni ne 26 or danniel chrischin ne 17 ran banaae
 While the top four batsmen could not even score double digit
 apane pehle hi ipel main shatak lagane vaale ben stokes ko main of da match se nawaja gaya
 Pune's wickets Sangwan took Ajinkya Rahane (4) for the fourth ball of the first over
 sangwan ne aakhri ball par pune ke captain steve smith (4) ko elbeadblu kar team ko do jatke die
 Basil Thampi dismissed Manoj Tiwari (0) lbw on the third ball of the next over
 chathe over main rahul treepathi doosraa ran lene kii koshish main ran out hue
 On the first ball of the 17th over, Dhoni became the victim of Basil Thampi
 gujarat kii ore se sangwan or basil thampi ne 2-2 wicket liye
 Gujarat's innings before losing the toss and batting first Gujarat's team 19
 5 over main 161 ranon par ol out ho gai or pune kii team ko jeet ke liye 162 ranon kaa lakshya diya
 For Gujarat, Brandon mccullum gave the team a quick start by scoring 45 runs off 27 balls and Ishan Kishan scored 31 off 24 balls
 haalanki imran taahir or jayadev unadakat ne 3-3 wicket lekar gujarat ke ranon par lagaam lagaai
 Apart from Tahir, Shardul Thakur took 1 wicket
 gujarat ke viketsgujrat ko pehla jhatka imran taahir ne diya
 He had Ishaan Kishan (31) caught by Washington Sundar
 team ko doosraa bada jhatka captain suresh raina (8) ke rup main laga
 Raina runs out trying to take the last ball of the eighth over
 10wein over kii aakhri do bolon par imran taahir ne gujarat ke 2 wicket chatkaaye
 On the 5th ball, he bowled Arane Finch for a cot and bowled, while on the sixth ball, Dwayne Smith was clean bowled
 team ko 5waan jhatka shardul thakur ne diya
 Rahane was caught in an attempt to play the 5th ball of the 12th over towards mccullum cover
 vahiin 15wein over kii aakhri ball par chrischin ne jadeja ko jayadev ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 In the 18th over, Jaydev Unadkat gave 2 shocks to Gujarat
 over kii duusari ball par unhone james foconor ko manoj tiwari ke haathon kaich karya to vahiin pi sangwan ko rahul treepathi ke haathon kaich karaayaa
